	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "その事実を。",
			NULL, "As he told us...", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//r私たちに、…告げた……。
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "私たちに、…告げた……。",
			NULL, "One... thing...", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DrawScene("background/ke_keijika1_02", 1000 );
	ModDrawCharacter(3, 31, "sprite/huji_sakebi_", "2", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 20, 200, TRUE );

//藤田rvS08/31/320900067.「南井警部が、垣内サービスエリア内で刺されました…。kvS08/31/320900068.出血多量で、…現在、危篤状態ですっ！！」
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#54636b>藤田</color>", NULL, "<color=#54636b>Fujita</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 31, "ps3/s08/31/320900067", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「南井警部が、垣内サービスエリア内で刺されました…。",
			NULL, "\"Chief Inspector Minai was stabbed at the Kakiuchi service area...", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 31, "ps3/s08/31/320900068", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "出血多量で、…現在、危篤状態ですっ！！」",
			NULL, " She was found bleeding heavily... and she's currently in critical condition!!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DisableWindow();
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 3000 );
	DrawBustshotWithFiltering(6, "cinema", "x", 1, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 1300, TRUE );
	DrawBustshot(7, "title02", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 26, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 2000 );
	DrawBustshot(5, "black", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	FadeBustshotWithFiltering( 7, "x", 1, FALSE, 0, 0, 1000, TRUE );
	DrawScene("black", 3000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

}
